<s> your friendship sir delights me <\s>
<s> your admiration for my girl brings tears to me eyes tears sir manlee tears and when she leaves me humble home for your own more splendid mansion i hope she'll keep a place for her poor old father poor old jack costigan the captain suited the action to the word and his bloodshot eyes were suffused with water as he addressed the major <\s>
<s> your sentiments do you honour the other said <\s>
<s> but captain costigan i can't help smiling at one thing you have just said <\s>
<s> and what's that sir <\s>
<s> asked jack who was at a too heroic and sentimental pitch to descend from it <\s>
<s> you were speaking about our splendid mansion my sister's house i mean <\s>
<s> i mane the park and mansion of arthur pendennis esquire of fairoaks park whom i hope to see a mimber of parliament for his native town of clavering when he is of ege to take that responsible stetion cried the captain with much dignity <\s>
<s> the major smiled as he recognised a shaft of his own bow <\s>
<s> it was he who had set pen upon the idea of sitting in parliament for the neighbouring borough and the poor lad had evidently been bragging on the subject to costigan and the lady of his affections <\s>
<s> fairoaks park my dear sir he said <\s>
<s> do you know our history <\s>
<s> we are of excessively ancient family certainly but i began life with scarce enough money to purchase my commission and my eldest brother was a country apothecary who made every shilling he died possessed of out of his pestle and mortar <\s>
<s> i have consented to waive that objection sir said costigan majestically in consideration of the known respectability of your family <\s>
<s> curse your impudence thought the major but he only smiled and bowed <\s>
<s> the costigans too have met with misfortunes and our house of castle costigan is by no manes what it was <\s>
<s> i have known very honest men apothecaries sir and there's some in dublin that has had the honour of dining at the lord leftenant's teeble <\s>
<s> you are very kind to give us the benefit of your charity the major continued but permit me to say that is not the question <\s>
<s> you spoke just now of my little nephew as heir of fairoaks park and i don't know what besides <\s>
<s> funded property i've no doubt meejor and something handsome eventually from yourself <\s>
<s> my good sir i tell you the boy is the son of a country apothecary cried out major pendennis and that when he comes of age he won't have a shilling <\s>
<s> pooh major you're laughing at me said mr <\s>
<s> costigan me young friend i make no doubt is heir to two thousand pounds a year <\s>
<s> i beg your pardon my dear sir but has the boy been humbugging you it is not his habit <\s>
<s> upon my word and honour as a gentleman and an executor to my brother's will too he left little more than five hundred a year behind him <\s>
<s> and with aconomy a handsome sum of money too sir the captain answered <\s>
<s> faith i've known a man drink his clar't and drive his coach and four on five hundred a year and strict aconomy in ireland sir <\s>
<s> we'll manage on it sir trust jack costigan for that <\s>
<s> my dear captain costigan i give you my word that my brother did not leave a shilling to his son arthur <\s>
<s> are ye joking with me meejor pendennis <\s>
<s> are ye thrifling with the feelings of a father and a gentleman <\s>
<s> i am telling you the honest truth said major pendennis <\s>
<s> every shilling my brother had he left to his widow with a partial reversion it is true to the boy <\s>
<s> but she is a young woman and may marry if he offends her or she may outlive him for she comes of an uncommonly long lived family <\s>
<s> and i ask you as a gentleman and a man of the world what allowance can my sister mrs <\s>
<s> pendennis make to her son out of five hundred a year which is all her fortune that shall enable him to maintain himself and your daughter in the rank befitting such an accomplished young lady <\s>
<s> am i to understand sir that the young gentleman your nephew and whom i have fosthered and cherished as the son of me bosom is an imposther who has been thrifling with the affections of me beloved child <\s>
<s> exclaimed the general with an outbreak of wrath have you yourself been working upon the feelings of the young man's susceptible nature to injuice him to break off an engagement and with it me adored emily's heart <\s>
<s> have a care sir how you thrifle with the honour of john costigan <\s>
<s> if i thought any mortal man meant to do so be heavens i'd have his blood sir were he old or young <\s>
<s> cried out the major <\s>
<s> costigan can protect his own and his daughter's honour and will sir said the other <\s>
<s> look at that chest of dthrawers it contains heaps of letthers that that viper has addressed to that innocent child <\s>
<s> there's promises there sir enough to fill a bandbox with and when i have dragged the scoundthrel before the courts of law and shown up his perjury and his dishonour i have another remedy in yondther mahogany case sir which shall set me right sir with any individual ye mark me words major pendennis with any individual who has counselled your nephew to insult a soldier and a gentleman <\s>
<s> me daughter to be jilted and me grey hairs dishonoured by an apothecary's son <\s>
<s> by the laws of heaven sir i should like to see the man that shall do it <\s>
<s> i am to understand then that you threaten in the first place to publish the letters of a boy of eighteen to a woman of eight and twenty and afterwards to do me the honour of calling me out the major said still with perfect coolness <\s>
<s> you have described my intentions with perfect accuracy meejor pendennis answered the captain as he pulled his ragged whiskers over his chin <\s>
<s> well well these shall be the subjects of future arrangements but before we come to powder and ball my good sir do have the kindness to think with yourself in what earthly way i have injured you <\s>
<s> i have told you that my nephew is dependent upon his mother who has scarcely more than five hundred a year <\s>
<s> i have my own opinion of the correctness of that assertion said the captain <\s>
<s> will you go to my sister's lawyers messrs <\s>
<s> tatham here and satisfy yourself <\s>
<s> i decline to meet those gentlemen said the captain with rather a disturbed air <\s>
<s> if it be as you say i have been athrociously deceived by some one and on that person i'll be revenged <\s>
<s> is it my nephew <\s>
<s> cried the major starting up and putting on his hat <\s>
<s> did he ever tell you that his property was two thousand a year <\s>
<s> if he did i'm mistaken in the boy <\s>
<s> to tell lies has not been a habit in our family mr <\s>
<s> costigan and i don't think my brother's son has learned it as yet <\s>
<s> try and consider whether you have not deceived yourself or adopted extravagant reports from hearsay as for me sir you are at liberty to understand that i am not afraid of all the costigans in ireland and know quite well how to defend myself against any threats from any quarter <\s>
<s> i come here as the boy's guardian to protest against a marriage most absurd and unequal that cannot but bring poverty and misery with it and in preventing it i conceive i am quite as much your daughter's friend who i have no doubt is an honourable young lady as the friend of my own family and prevent the marriage i will sir by every means in my power <\s>
<s> there i have said my say sir <\s>
<s> but i have not said mine major pendennis and ye shall hear more from me mr <\s>
<s> costigan said with a look of tremendous severity <\s>
<s> sdeath sir what do you mean <\s>

<s> ye said in the coorse of conversation that ye were at the george hotel i think mr <\s>
<s> costigan said in a stately manner <\s>
<s> a friend shall wait upon ye there before ye leave town sir <\s>
<s> let him make haste mr <\s>
<s> costigan cried out the major almost beside himself with rage <\s>
<s> i wish you a good morning sir <\s>
<s> and captain costigan bowed a magnificent bow of defiance to major pendennis over the landing place as the latter retreated down the stairs <\s>

<s> arthur pendennis and his daughter miss fotheringay and to fix an early day for its celebration or in any other case to give him the satisfaction which was usual between gentlemen of honour <\s>

<s> captain costigan did not disclose to him the whole of the previous events of which the reader is in possession but with the aid of the spirits and water he composed a letter of a threatening nature to major pendennis's address in which he called upon that gentleman to offer no hindrance to the marriage projected between mr <\s>
<s> arthur pendennis and his daughter miss fotheringay and to fix an early day for its celebration or in any other case to give him the satisfaction which was usual between gentlemen of honour <\s>
<s> and should major pendennis be disinclined to this alternative the captain hinted that he would force him to accept by the use of a horsewhip which he should employ upon the major's person <\s>
<s> the precise terms of this letter we cannot give for reasons which shall be specified presently but it was no doubt couched in the captain's finest style and sealed elaborately with the great silver seal of the costigans the only bit of the family plate which the captain possessed <\s>
<s> garbetts was despatched then with this message and letter and bidding heaven bless um the general squeezed his ambassador's hand and saw him depart <\s>
<s> then he took down his venerable and murderous duelling pistols with flint locks that had done the business of many a pretty fellow in dublin and having examined these and seen that they were in a satisfactory condition he brought from the drawer all pen's letters and poems which he kept there and which he always read before he permitted his emily to enjoy their perusal <\s>

<s> you were speaking about our splendid mansion my sister's house i mean <\s>

<s> do you know our history <\s>
<s> we are of excessively ancient family certainly but i began life with scarce enough money to purchase my commission and my eldest brother was a country apothecary who made every shilling he died possessed of out of his pestle and mortar <\s>
<s> i have consented to waive that objection sir said costigan majestically in consideration of the known respectability of your family <\s>

<s> we are of excessively ancient family certainly but i began life with scarce enough money to purchase my commission and my eldest brother was a country apothecary who made every shilling he died possessed of out of his pestle and mortar <\s>
<s> i have consented to waive that objection sir said costigan majestically in consideration of the known respectability of your family <\s>
<s> curse your impudence thought the major but he only smiled and bowed <\s>
<s> the costigans too have met with misfortunes and our house of castle costigan is by no manes what it was <\s>
<s> i have known very honest men apothecaries sir and there's some in dublin that has had the honour of dining at the lord leftenant's teeble <\s>
<s> you are very kind to give us the benefit of your charity the major continued but permit me to say that is not the question <\s>
<s> you spoke just now of my little nephew as heir of fairoaks park and i don't know what besides <\s>
<s> funded property i've no doubt meejor and something handsome eventually from yourself <\s>
<s> my good sir i tell you the boy is the son of a country apothecary cried out major pendennis and that when he comes of age he won't have a shilling <\s>
<s> pooh major you're laughing at me said mr <\s>
<s> costigan me young friend i make no doubt is heir to two thousand pounds a year <\s>
<s> i beg your pardon my dear sir but has the boy been humbugging you it is not his habit <\s>
<s> upon my word and honour as a gentleman and an executor to my brother's will too he left little more than five hundred a year behind him <\s>
<s> and with aconomy a handsome sum of money too sir the captain answered <\s>
<s> faith i've known a man drink his clar't and drive his coach and four on five hundred a year and strict aconomy in ireland sir <\s>
<s> we'll manage on it sir trust jack costigan for that <\s>
<s> my dear captain costigan i give you my word that my brother did not leave a shilling to his son arthur <\s>
<s> are ye joking with me meejor pendennis <\s>
<s> are ye thrifling with the feelings of a father and a gentleman <\s>
<s> i am telling you the honest truth said major pendennis <\s>
<s> every shilling my brother had he left to his widow with a partial reversion it is true to the boy <\s>
<s> but she is a young woman and may marry if he offends her or she may outlive him for she comes of an uncommonly long lived family <\s>
<s> and i ask you as a gentleman and a man of the world what allowance can my sister mrs <\s>
<s> pendennis make to her son out of five hundred a year which is all her fortune that shall enable him to maintain himself and your daughter in the rank befitting such an accomplished young lady <\s>
<s> am i to understand sir that the young gentleman your nephew and whom i have fosthered and cherished as the son of me bosom is an imposther who has been thrifling with the affections of me beloved child <\s>
<s> exclaimed the general with an outbreak of wrath have you yourself been working upon the feelings of the young man's susceptible nature to injuice him to break off an engagement and with it me adored emily's heart <\s>
<s> have a care sir how you thrifle with the honour of john costigan <\s>
<s> if i thought any mortal man meant to do so be heavens i'd have his blood sir were he old or young <\s>
<s> cried out the major <\s>
<s> costigan can protect his own and his daughter's honour and will sir said the other <\s>
<s> look at that chest of dthrawers it contains heaps of letthers that that viper has addressed to that innocent child <\s>
<s> there's promises there sir enough to fill a bandbox with and when i have dragged the scoundthrel before the courts of law and shown up his perjury and his dishonour i have another remedy in yondther mahogany case sir which shall set me right sir with any individual ye mark me words major pendennis with any individual who has counselled your nephew to insult a soldier and a gentleman <\s>
<s> me daughter to be jilted and me grey hairs dishonoured by an apothecary's son <\s>
<s> by the laws of heaven sir i should like to see the man that shall do it <\s>
<s> i am to understand then that you threaten in the first place to publish the letters of a boy of eighteen to a woman of eight and twenty and afterwards to do me the honour of calling me out the major said still with perfect coolness <\s>
<s> you have described my intentions with perfect accuracy meejor pendennis answered the captain as he pulled his ragged whiskers over his chin <\s>
<s> well well these shall be the subjects of future arrangements but before we come to powder and ball my good sir do have the kindness to think with yourself in what earthly way i have injured you <\s>
<s> i have told you that my nephew is dependent upon his mother who has scarcely more than five hundred a year <\s>
<s> i have my own opinion of the correctness of that assertion said the captain <\s>
<s> will you go to my sister's lawyers messrs <\s>
<s> tatham here and satisfy yourself <\s>
<s> i decline to meet those gentlemen said the captain with rather a disturbed air <\s>
<s> if it be as you say i have been athrociously deceived by some one and on that person i'll be revenged <\s>
<s> is it my nephew <\s>
<s> cried the major starting up and putting on his hat <\s>
<s> did he ever tell you that his property was two thousand a year <\s>
<s> if he did i'm mistaken in the boy <\s>
<s> to tell lies has not been a habit in our family mr <\s>
<s> costigan and i don't think my brother's son has learned it as yet <\s>
<s> try and consider whether you have not deceived yourself or adopted extravagant reports from hearsay as for me sir you are at liberty to understand that i am not afraid of all the costigans in ireland and know quite well how to defend myself against any threats from any quarter <\s>
<s> i come here as the boy's guardian to protest against a marriage most absurd and unequal that cannot but bring poverty and misery with it and in preventing it i conceive i am quite as much your daughter's friend who i have no doubt is an honourable young lady as the friend of my own family and prevent the marriage i will sir by every means in my power <\s>
<s> there i have said my say sir <\s>
<s> but i have not said mine major pendennis and ye shall hear more from me mr <\s>
<s> costigan said with a look of tremendous severity <\s>
<s> sdeath sir what do you mean <\s>
<s> the major asked turning round on the threshold of the door and looking the intrepid costigan in the face <\s>
<s> ye said in the coorse of conversation that ye were at the george hotel i think mr <\s>
<s> costigan said in a stately manner <\s>
<s> a friend shall wait upon ye there before ye leave town sir <\s>
<s> let him make haste mr <\s>
<s> costigan cried out the major almost beside himself with rage <\s>
<s> i wish you a good morning sir <\s>
<s> and captain costigan bowed a magnificent bow of defiance to major pendennis over the landing place as the latter retreated down the stairs <\s>

<s> costigan there was a considerable intimacy <\s>

<s> they were friends in fine although mr <\s>
<s> garbetts seldom called at costigan's house being disliked by miss fotheringay of whom in her turn mrs <\s>

<s> garbetts and the whisky came <\s>
<s> captain costigan did not disclose to him the whole of the previous events of which the reader is in possession but with the aid of the spirits and water he composed a letter of a threatening nature to major pendennis's address in which he called upon that gentleman to offer no hindrance to the marriage projected between mr <\s>
<s> arthur pendennis and his daughter miss fotheringay and to fix an early day for its celebration or in any other case to give him the satisfaction which was usual between gentlemen of honour <\s>
<s> and should major pendennis be disinclined to this alternative the captain hinted that he would force him to accept by the use of a horsewhip which he should employ upon the major's person <\s>
<s> the precise terms of this letter we cannot give for reasons which shall be specified presently but it was no doubt couched in the captain's finest style and sealed elaborately with the great silver seal of the costigans the only bit of the family plate which the captain possessed <\s>
<s> garbetts was despatched then with this message and letter and bidding heaven bless um the general squeezed his ambassador's hand and saw him depart <\s>
<s> then he took down his venerable and murderous duelling pistols with flint locks that had done the business of many a pretty fellow in dublin and having examined these and seen that they were in a satisfactory condition he brought from the drawer all pen's letters and poems which he kept there and which he always read before he permitted his emily to enjoy their perusal <\s>

<s> captain costigan did not disclose to him the whole of the previous events of which the reader is in possession but with the aid of the spirits and water he composed a letter of a threatening nature to major pendennis's address in which he called upon that gentleman to offer no hindrance to the marriage projected between mr <\s>
<s> arthur pendennis and his daughter miss fotheringay and to fix an early day for its celebration or in any other case to give him the satisfaction which was usual between gentlemen of honour <\s>
<s> and should major pendennis be disinclined to this alternative the captain hinted that he would force him to accept by the use of a horsewhip which he should employ upon the major's person <\s>
<s> the precise terms of this letter we cannot give for reasons which shall be specified presently but it was no doubt couched in the captain's finest style and sealed elaborately with the great silver seal of the costigans the only bit of the family plate which the captain possessed <\s>
<s> garbetts was despatched then with this message and letter and bidding heaven bless um the general squeezed his ambassador's hand and saw him depart <\s>
<s> then he took down his venerable and murderous duelling pistols with flint locks that had done the business of many a pretty fellow in dublin and having examined these and seen that they were in a satisfactory condition he brought from the drawer all pen's letters and poems which he kept there and which he always read before he permitted his emily to enjoy their perusal <\s>
<s> in a score of minutes garbetts came back with an anxious and crestfallen countenance <\s>
<s> why yes said garbetts <\s>
<s> your friendship sir delights me <\s>
<s> your admiration for my girl brings tears to me eyes tears sir manlee tears and when she leaves me humble home for your own more splendid mansion i hope she'll keep a place for her poor old father poor old jack costigan the captain suited the action to the word and his bloodshot eyes were suffused with water as he addressed the major <\s>

<s> but captain costigan i can't help smiling at one thing you have just said <\s>
<s> and what's that sir <\s>
<s> asked jack who was at a too heroic and sentimental pitch to descend from it <\s>
<s> you were speaking about our splendid mansion my sister's house i mean <\s>
<s> i mane the park and mansion of arthur pendennis esquire of fairoaks park whom i hope to see a mimber of parliament for his native town of clavering when he is of ege to take that responsible stetion cried the captain with much dignity <\s>
<s> the major smiled as he recognised a shaft of his own bow <\s>
<s> it was he who had set pen upon the idea of sitting in parliament for the neighbouring borough and the poor lad had evidently been bragging on the subject to costigan and the lady of his affections <\s>
<s> fairoaks park my dear sir he said <\s>
<s> do you know our history <\s>
<s> we are of excessively ancient family certainly but i began life with scarce enough money to purchase my commission and my eldest brother was a country apothecary who made every shilling he died possessed of out of his pestle and mortar <\s>
<s> i have consented to waive that objection sir said costigan majestically in consideration of the known respectability of your family <\s>
<s> curse your impudence thought the major but he only smiled and bowed <\s>
<s> the costigans too have met with misfortunes and our house of castle costigan is by no manes what it was <\s>
<s> i have known very honest men apothecaries sir and there's some in dublin that has had the honour of dining at the lord leftenant's teeble <\s>
<s> you are very kind to give us the benefit of your charity the major continued but permit me to say that is not the question <\s>
<s> you spoke just now of my little nephew as heir of fairoaks park and i don't know what besides <\s>
<s> funded property i've no doubt meejor and something handsome eventually from yourself <\s>
<s> my good sir i tell you the boy is the son of a country apothecary cried out major pendennis and that when he comes of age he won't have a shilling <\s>
<s> pooh major you're laughing at me said mr <\s>
<s> costigan me young friend i make no doubt is heir to two thousand pounds a year <\s>
<s> i beg your pardon my dear sir but has the boy been humbugging you it is not his habit <\s>
<s> upon my word and honour as a gentleman and an executor to my brother's will too he left little more than five hundred a year behind him <\s>
<s> and with aconomy a handsome sum of money too sir the captain answered <\s>

<s> we'll manage on it sir trust jack costigan for that <\s>
<s> my dear captain costigan i give you my word that my brother did not leave a shilling to his son arthur <\s>
<s> are ye joking with me meejor pendennis <\s>
<s> are ye thrifling with the feelings of a father and a gentleman <\s>
<s> i am telling you the honest truth said major pendennis <\s>
<s> every shilling my brother had he left to his widow with a partial reversion it is true to the boy <\s>
<s> but she is a young woman and may marry if he offends her or she may outlive him for she comes of an uncommonly long lived family <\s>
<s> and i ask you as a gentleman and a man of the world what allowance can my sister mrs <\s>
<s> pendennis make to her son out of five hundred a year which is all her fortune that shall enable him to maintain himself and your daughter in the rank befitting such an accomplished young lady <\s>
<s> am i to understand sir that the young gentleman your nephew and whom i have fosthered and cherished as the son of me bosom is an imposther who has been thrifling with the affections of me beloved child <\s>
<s> exclaimed the general with an outbreak of wrath have you yourself been working upon the feelings of the young man's susceptible nature to injuice him to break off an engagement and with it me adored emily's heart <\s>
<s> have a care sir how you thrifle with the honour of john costigan <\s>

<s> cried out the major <\s>

<s> me daughter to be jilted and me grey hairs dishonoured by an apothecary's son <\s>
<s> by the laws of heaven sir i should like to see the man that shall do it <\s>

<s> you have described my intentions with perfect accuracy meejor pendennis answered the captain as he pulled his ragged whiskers over his chin <\s>

<s> me daughter to be jilted and me grey hairs dishonoured by an apothecary's son <\s>
<s> by the laws of heaven sir i should like to see the man that shall do it <\s>
<s> i am to understand then that you threaten in the first place to publish the letters of a boy of eighteen to a woman of eight and twenty and afterwards to do me the honour of calling me out the major said still with perfect coolness <\s>
<s> you have described my intentions with perfect accuracy meejor pendennis answered the captain as he pulled his ragged whiskers over his chin <\s>
<s> well well these shall be the subjects of future arrangements but before we come to powder and ball my good sir do have the kindness to think with yourself in what earthly way i have injured you <\s>

<s> tatham here and satisfy yourself <\s>

<s> is it my nephew <\s>
<s> cried the major starting up and putting on his hat <\s>

<s> costigan and i don't think my brother's son has learned it as yet <\s>

<s> i come here as the boy's guardian to protest against a marriage most absurd and unequal that cannot but bring poverty and misery with it and in preventing it i conceive i am quite as much your daughter's friend who i have no doubt is an honourable young lady as the friend of my own family and prevent the marriage i will sir by every means in my power <\s>

<s> costigan said in a stately manner <\s>

<s> costigan cried out the major almost beside himself with rage <\s>
<s> i wish you a good morning sir <\s>

<s> captain costigan did not disclose to him the whole of the previous events of which the reader is in possession but with the aid of the spirits and water he composed a letter of a threatening nature to major pendennis's address in which he called upon that gentleman to offer no hindrance to the marriage projected between mr <\s>
<s> arthur pendennis and his daughter miss fotheringay and to fix an early day for its celebration or in any other case to give him the satisfaction which was usual between gentlemen of honour <\s>
<s> and should major pendennis be disinclined to this alternative the captain hinted that he would force him to accept by the use of a horsewhip which he should employ upon the major's person <\s>

<s> captain costigan did not disclose to him the whole of the previous events of which the reader is in possession but with the aid of the spirits and water he composed a letter of a threatening nature to major pendennis's address in which he called upon that gentleman to offer no hindrance to the marriage projected between mr <\s>
<s> arthur pendennis and his daughter miss fotheringay and to fix an early day for its celebration or in any other case to give him the satisfaction which was usual between gentlemen of honour <\s>
<s> and should major pendennis be disinclined to this alternative the captain hinted that he would force him to accept by the use of a horsewhip which he should employ upon the major's person <\s>
<s> the precise terms of this letter we cannot give for reasons which shall be specified presently but it was no doubt couched in the captain's finest style and sealed elaborately with the great silver seal of the costigans the only bit of the family plate which the captain possessed <\s>
<s> garbetts was despatched then with this message and letter and bidding heaven bless um the general squeezed his ambassador's hand and saw him depart <\s>
<s> then he took down his venerable and murderous duelling pistols with flint locks that had done the business of many a pretty fellow in dublin and having examined these and seen that they were in a satisfactory condition he brought from the drawer all pen's letters and poems which he kept there and which he always read before he permitted his emily to enjoy their perusal <\s>

<s> do you know our history <\s>
<s> we are of excessively ancient family certainly but i began life with scarce enough money to purchase my commission and my eldest brother was a country apothecary who made every shilling he died possessed of out of his pestle and mortar <\s>
<s> i have consented to waive that objection sir said costigan majestically in consideration of the known respectability of your family <\s>
<s> curse your impudence thought the major but he only smiled and bowed <\s>
<s> the costigans too have met with misfortunes and our house of castle costigan is by no manes what it was <\s>
<s> i have known very honest men apothecaries sir and there's some in dublin that has had the honour of dining at the lord leftenant's teeble <\s>
<s> you are very kind to give us the benefit of your charity the major continued but permit me to say that is not the question <\s>
<s> you spoke just now of my little nephew as heir of fairoaks park and i don't know what besides <\s>
<s> funded property i've no doubt meejor and something handsome eventually from yourself <\s>
<s> my good sir i tell you the boy is the son of a country apothecary cried out major pendennis and that when he comes of age he won't have a shilling <\s>
<s> pooh major you're laughing at me said mr <\s>
<s> costigan me young friend i make no doubt is heir to two thousand pounds a year <\s>
<s> i beg your pardon my dear sir but has the boy been humbugging you it is not his habit <\s>
<s> upon my word and honour as a gentleman and an executor to my brother's will too he left little more than five hundred a year behind him <\s>
<s> and with aconomy a handsome sum of money too sir the captain answered <\s>

<s> we'll manage on it sir trust jack costigan for that <\s>
<s> my dear captain costigan i give you my word that my brother did not leave a shilling to his son arthur <\s>

<s> are ye thrifling with the feelings of a father and a gentleman <\s>
<s> i am telling you the honest truth said major pendennis <\s>

<s> but she is a young woman and may marry if he offends her or she may outlive him for she comes of an uncommonly long lived family <\s>
<s> and i ask you as a gentleman and a man of the world what allowance can my sister mrs <\s>
<s> pendennis make to her son out of five hundred a year which is all her fortune that shall enable him to maintain himself and your daughter in the rank befitting such an accomplished young lady <\s>
<s> am i to understand sir that the young gentleman your nephew and whom i have fosthered and cherished as the son of me bosom is an imposther who has been thrifling with the affections of me beloved child <\s>
<s> exclaimed the general with an outbreak of wrath have you yourself been working upon the feelings of the young man's susceptible nature to injuice him to break off an engagement and with it me adored emily's heart <\s>
<s> have a care sir how you thrifle with the honour of john costigan <\s>

<s> cried out the major <\s>

<s> me daughter to be jilted and me grey hairs dishonoured by an apothecary's son <\s>
<s> by the laws of heaven sir i should like to see the man that shall do it <\s>

<s> you have described my intentions with perfect accuracy meejor pendennis answered the captain as he pulled his ragged whiskers over his chin <\s>
<s> well well these shall be the subjects of future arrangements but before we come to powder and ball my good sir do have the kindness to think with yourself in what earthly way i have injured you <\s>

<s> tatham here and satisfy yourself <\s>
<s> i decline to meet those gentlemen said the captain with rather a disturbed air <\s>

<s> is it my nephew <\s>
<s> cried the major starting up and putting on his hat <\s>
<s> did he ever tell you that his property was two thousand a year <\s>

<s> costigan and i don't think my brother's son has learned it as yet <\s>

<s> pendennis make to her son out of five hundred a year which is all her fortune that shall enable him to maintain himself and your daughter in the rank befitting such an accomplished young lady <\s>
<s> am i to understand sir that the young gentleman your nephew and whom i have fosthered and cherished as the son of me bosom is an imposther who has been thrifling with the affections of me beloved child <\s>
<s> exclaimed the general with an outbreak of wrath have you yourself been working upon the feelings of the young man's susceptible nature to injuice him to break off an engagement and with it me adored emily's heart <\s>
<s> have a care sir how you thrifle with the honour of john costigan <\s>
<s> if i thought any mortal man meant to do so be heavens i'd have his blood sir were he old or young <\s>
<s> cried out the major <\s>
<s> costigan can protect his own and his daughter's honour and will sir said the other <\s>
<s> look at that chest of dthrawers it contains heaps of letthers that that viper has addressed to that innocent child <\s>
<s> there's promises there sir enough to fill a bandbox with and when i have dragged the scoundthrel before the courts of law and shown up his perjury and his dishonour i have another remedy in yondther mahogany case sir which shall set me right sir with any individual ye mark me words major pendennis with any individual who has counselled your nephew to insult a soldier and a gentleman <\s>
<s> me daughter to be jilted and me grey hairs dishonoured by an apothecary's son <\s>
<s> by the laws of heaven sir i should like to see the man that shall do it <\s>
<s> i am to understand then that you threaten in the first place to publish the letters of a boy of eighteen to a woman of eight and twenty and afterwards to do me the honour of calling me out the major said still with perfect coolness <\s>
<s> you have described my intentions with perfect accuracy meejor pendennis answered the captain as he pulled his ragged whiskers over his chin <\s>
<s> well well these shall be the subjects of future arrangements but before we come to powder and ball my good sir do have the kindness to think with yourself in what earthly way i have injured you <\s>
<s> i have told you that my nephew is dependent upon his mother who has scarcely more than five hundred a year <\s>
<s> i have my own opinion of the correctness of that assertion said the captain <\s>
<s> will you go to my sister's lawyers messrs <\s>
<s> tatham here and satisfy yourself <\s>
<s> i decline to meet those gentlemen said the captain with rather a disturbed air <\s>
<s> if it be as you say i have been athrociously deceived by some one and on that person i'll be revenged <\s>
<s> is it my nephew <\s>
<s> cried the major starting up and putting on his hat <\s>
<s> did he ever tell you that his property was two thousand a year <\s>
<s> if he did i'm mistaken in the boy <\s>
<s> to tell lies has not been a habit in our family mr <\s>
<s> costigan and i don't think my brother's son has learned it as yet <\s>
<s> try and consider whether you have not deceived yourself or adopted extravagant reports from hearsay as for me sir you are at liberty to understand that i am not afraid of all the costigans in ireland and know quite well how to defend myself against any threats from any quarter <\s>
<s> i come here as the boy's guardian to protest against a marriage most absurd and unequal that cannot but bring poverty and misery with it and in preventing it i conceive i am quite as much your daughter's friend who i have no doubt is an honourable young lady as the friend of my own family and prevent the marriage i will sir by every means in my power <\s>
<s> there i have said my say sir <\s>
<s> but i have not said mine major pendennis and ye shall hear more from me mr <\s>
<s> costigan said with a look of tremendous severity <\s>
<s> sdeath sir what do you mean <\s>
<s> the major asked turning round on the threshold of the door and looking the intrepid costigan in the face <\s>
<s> ye said in the coorse of conversation that ye were at the george hotel i think mr <\s>
<s> costigan said in a stately manner <\s>
<s> a friend shall wait upon ye there before ye leave town sir <\s>
<s> let him make haste mr <\s>
<s> costigan cried out the major almost beside himself with rage <\s>
<s> i wish you a good morning sir <\s>
<s> and captain costigan bowed a magnificent bow of defiance to major pendennis over the landing place as the latter retreated down the stairs <\s>

<s> captain costigan did not disclose to him the whole of the previous events of which the reader is in possession but with the aid of the spirits and water he composed a letter of a threatening nature to major pendennis's address in which he called upon that gentleman to offer no hindrance to the marriage projected between mr <\s>
<s> arthur pendennis and his daughter miss fotheringay and to fix an early day for its celebration or in any other case to give him the satisfaction which was usual between gentlemen of honour <\s>
<s> and should major pendennis be disinclined to this alternative the captain hinted that he would force him to accept by the use of a horsewhip which he should employ upon the major's person <\s>
<s> the precise terms of this letter we cannot give for reasons which shall be specified presently but it was no doubt couched in the captain's finest style and sealed elaborately with the great silver seal of the costigans the only bit of the family plate which the captain possessed <\s>
<s> garbetts was despatched then with this message and letter and bidding heaven bless um the general squeezed his ambassador's hand and saw him depart <\s>
<s> then he took down his venerable and murderous duelling pistols with flint locks that had done the business of many a pretty fellow in dublin and having examined these and seen that they were in a satisfactory condition he brought from the drawer all pen's letters and poems which he kept there and which he always read before he permitted his emily to enjoy their perusal <\s>

<s> captain costigan did not disclose to him the whole of the previous events of which the reader is in possession but with the aid of the spirits and water he composed a letter of a threatening nature to major pendennis's address in which he called upon that gentleman to offer no hindrance to the marriage projected between mr <\s>
<s> arthur pendennis and his daughter miss fotheringay and to fix an early day for its celebration or in any other case to give him the satisfaction which was usual between gentlemen of honour <\s>
<s> and should major pendennis be disinclined to this alternative the captain hinted that he would force him to accept by the use of a horsewhip which he should employ upon the major's person <\s>
<s> the precise terms of this letter we cannot give for reasons which shall be specified presently but it was no doubt couched in the captain's finest style and sealed elaborately with the great silver seal of the costigans the only bit of the family plate which the captain possessed <\s>
<s> garbetts was despatched then with this message and letter and bidding heaven bless um the general squeezed his ambassador's hand and saw him depart <\s>
<s> then he took down his venerable and murderous duelling pistols with flint locks that had done the business of many a pretty fellow in dublin and having examined these and seen that they were in a satisfactory condition he brought from the drawer all pen's letters and poems which he kept there and which he always read before he permitted his emily to enjoy their perusal <\s>

<s> why yes said garbetts <\s>
<s> your friendship sir delights me <\s>

<s> asked jack who was at a too heroic and sentimental pitch to descend from it <\s>
<s> you were speaking about our splendid mansion my sister's house i mean <\s>

<s> it was he who had set pen upon the idea of sitting in parliament for the neighbouring borough and the poor lad had evidently been bragging on the subject to costigan and the lady of his affections <\s>
<s> fairoaks park my dear sir he said <\s>
<s> do you know our history <\s>
<s> we are of excessively ancient family certainly but i began life with scarce enough money to purchase my commission and my eldest brother was a country apothecary who made every shilling he died possessed of out of his pestle and mortar <\s>
<s> i have consented to waive that objection sir said costigan majestically in consideration of the known respectability of your family <\s>
<s> curse your impudence thought the major but he only smiled and bowed <\s>
<s> the costigans too have met with misfortunes and our house of castle costigan is by no manes what it was <\s>
<s> i have known very honest men apothecaries sir and there's some in dublin that has had the honour of dining at the lord leftenant's teeble <\s>
<s> you are very kind to give us the benefit of your charity the major continued but permit me to say that is not the question <\s>
<s> you spoke just now of my little nephew as heir of fairoaks park and i don't know what besides <\s>
<s> funded property i've no doubt meejor and something handsome eventually from yourself <\s>
<s> my good sir i tell you the boy is the son of a country apothecary cried out major pendennis and that when he comes of age he won't have a shilling <\s>
<s> pooh major you're laughing at me said mr <\s>
<s> costigan me young friend i make no doubt is heir to two thousand pounds a year <\s>
<s> i beg your pardon my dear sir but has the boy been humbugging you it is not his habit <\s>
<s> upon my word and honour as a gentleman and an executor to my brother's will too he left little more than five hundred a year behind him <\s>
<s> and with aconomy a handsome sum of money too sir the captain answered <\s>

<s> we'll manage on it sir trust jack costigan for that <\s>
<s> my dear captain costigan i give you my word that my brother did not leave a shilling to his son arthur <\s>
<s> are ye joking with me meejor pendennis <\s>
<s> are ye thrifling with the feelings of a father and a gentleman <\s>
<s> i am telling you the honest truth said major pendennis <\s>
<s> every shilling my brother had he left to his widow with a partial reversion it is true to the boy <\s>
<s> but she is a young woman and may marry if he offends her or she may outlive him for she comes of an uncommonly long lived family <\s>
<s> and i ask you as a gentleman and a man of the world what allowance can my sister mrs <\s>
<s> pendennis make to her son out of five hundred a year which is all her fortune that shall enable him to maintain himself and your daughter in the rank befitting such an accomplished young lady <\s>
<s> am i to understand sir that the young gentleman your nephew and whom i have fosthered and cherished as the son of me bosom is an imposther who has been thrifling with the affections of me beloved child <\s>
<s> exclaimed the general with an outbreak of wrath have you yourself been working upon the feelings of the young man's susceptible nature to injuice him to break off an engagement and with it me adored emily's heart <\s>
<s> have a care sir how you thrifle with the honour of john costigan <\s>
<s> if i thought any mortal man meant to do so be heavens i'd have his blood sir were he old or young <\s>
<s> cried out the major <\s>
<s> costigan can protect his own and his daughter's honour and will sir said the other <\s>
<s> look at that chest of dthrawers it contains heaps of letthers that that viper has addressed to that innocent child <\s>
<s> there's promises there sir enough to fill a bandbox with and when i have dragged the scoundthrel before the courts of law and shown up his perjury and his dishonour i have another remedy in yondther mahogany case sir which shall set me right sir with any individual ye mark me words major pendennis with any individual who has counselled your nephew to insult a soldier and a gentleman <\s>
<s> me daughter to be jilted and me grey hairs dishonoured by an apothecary's son <\s>
<s> by the laws of heaven sir i should like to see the man that shall do it <\s>
<s> i am to understand then that you threaten in the first place to publish the letters of a boy of eighteen to a woman of eight and twenty and afterwards to do me the honour of calling me out the major said still with perfect coolness <\s>
<s> you have described my intentions with perfect accuracy meejor pendennis answered the captain as he pulled his ragged whiskers over his chin <\s>
<s> well well these shall be the subjects of future arrangements but before we come to powder and ball my good sir do have the kindness to think with yourself in what earthly way i have injured you <\s>
<s> i have told you that my nephew is dependent upon his mother who has scarcely more than five hundred a year <\s>
<s> i have my own opinion of the correctness of that assertion said the captain <\s>
<s> will you go to my sister's lawyers messrs <\s>
<s> tatham here and satisfy yourself <\s>
<s> i decline to meet those gentlemen said the captain with rather a disturbed air <\s>
<s> if it be as you say i have been athrociously deceived by some one and on that person i'll be revenged <\s>
<s> is it my nephew <\s>
<s> cried the major starting up and putting on his hat <\s>
<s> did he ever tell you that his property was two thousand a year <\s>
<s> if he did i'm mistaken in the boy <\s>
<s> to tell lies has not been a habit in our family mr <\s>
<s> costigan and i don't think my brother's son has learned it as yet <\s>
<s> try and consider whether you have not deceived yourself or adopted extravagant reports from hearsay as for me sir you are at liberty to understand that i am not afraid of all the costigans in ireland and know quite well how to defend myself against any threats from any quarter <\s>
<s> i come here as the boy's guardian to protest against a marriage most absurd and unequal that cannot but bring poverty and misery with it and in preventing it i conceive i am quite as much your daughter's friend who i have no doubt is an honourable young lady as the friend of my own family and prevent the marriage i will sir by every means in my power <\s>
<s> there i have said my say sir <\s>
<s> but i have not said mine major pendennis and ye shall hear more from me mr <\s>

<s> i am to understand then that you threaten in the first place to publish the letters of a boy of eighteen to a woman of eight and twenty and afterwards to do me the honour of calling me out the major said still with perfect coolness <\s>
<s> you have described my intentions with perfect accuracy meejor pendennis answered the captain as he pulled his ragged whiskers over his chin <\s>
<s> well well these shall be the subjects of future arrangements but before we come to powder and ball my good sir do have the kindness to think with yourself in what earthly way i have injured you <\s>

<s> tatham here and satisfy yourself <\s>

<s> captain costigan did not disclose to him the whole of the previous events of which the reader is in possession but with the aid of the spirits and water he composed a letter of a threatening nature to major pendennis's address in which he called upon that gentleman to offer no hindrance to the marriage projected between mr <\s>
<s> arthur pendennis and his daughter miss fotheringay and to fix an early day for its celebration or in any other case to give him the satisfaction which was usual between gentlemen of honour <\s>
<s> and should major pendennis be disinclined to this alternative the captain hinted that he would force him to accept by the use of a horsewhip which he should employ upon the major's person <\s>
<s> the precise terms of this letter we cannot give for reasons which shall be specified presently but it was no doubt couched in the captain's finest style and sealed elaborately with the great silver seal of the costigans the only bit of the family plate which the captain possessed <\s>
<s> garbetts was despatched then with this message and letter and bidding heaven bless um the general squeezed his ambassador's hand and saw him depart <\s>

<s> then he took down his venerable and murderous duelling pistols with flint locks that had done the business of many a pretty fellow in dublin and having examined these and seen that they were in a satisfactory condition he brought from the drawer all pen's letters and poems which he kept there and which he always read before he permitted his emily to enjoy their perusal <\s>
<s> in a score of minutes garbetts came back with an anxious and crestfallen countenance <\s>
<s> why yes said garbetts <\s>
<s> your friendship sir delights me <\s>
<s> your admiration for my girl brings tears to me eyes tears sir manlee tears and when she leaves me humble home for your own more splendid mansion i hope she'll keep a place for her poor old father poor old jack costigan the captain suited the action to the word and his bloodshot eyes were suffused with water as he addressed the major <\s>
<s> your sentiments do you honour the other said <\s>
<s> but captain costigan i can't help smiling at one thing you have just said <\s>
<s> and what's that sir <\s>
<s> asked jack who was at a too heroic and sentimental pitch to descend from it <\s>
<s> you were speaking about our splendid mansion my sister's house i mean <\s>
<s> i mane the park and mansion of arthur pendennis esquire of fairoaks park whom i hope to see a mimber of parliament for his native town of clavering when he is of ege to take that responsible stetion cried the captain with much dignity <\s>
<s> the major smiled as he recognised a shaft of his own bow <\s>
<s> it was he who had set pen upon the idea of sitting in parliament for the neighbouring borough and the poor lad had evidently been bragging on the subject to costigan and the lady of his affections <\s>
<s> fairoaks park my dear sir he said <\s>
<s> do you know our history <\s>
<s> we are of excessively ancient family certainly but i began life with scarce enough money to purchase my commission and my eldest brother was a country apothecary who made every shilling he died possessed of out of his pestle and mortar <\s>
<s> i have consented to waive that objection sir said costigan majestically in consideration of the known respectability of your family <\s>
<s> curse your impudence thought the major but he only smiled and bowed <\s>
<s> the costigans too have met with misfortunes and our house of castle costigan is by no manes what it was <\s>
<s> i have known very honest men apothecaries sir and there's some in dublin that has had the honour of dining at the lord leftenant's teeble <\s>
<s> you are very kind to give us the benefit of your charity the major continued but permit me to say that is not the question <\s>
<s> you spoke just now of my little nephew as heir of fairoaks park and i don't know what besides <\s>
<s> funded property i've no doubt meejor and something handsome eventually from yourself <\s>
<s> my good sir i tell you the boy is the son of a country apothecary cried out major pendennis and that when he comes of age he won't have a shilling <\s>
<s> pooh major you're laughing at me said mr <\s>
<s> costigan me young friend i make no doubt is heir to two thousand pounds a year <\s>
<s> i beg your pardon my dear sir but has the boy been humbugging you it is not his habit <\s>
<s> upon my word and honour as a gentleman and an executor to my brother's will too he left little more than five hundred a year behind him <\s>
<s> and with aconomy a handsome sum of money too sir the captain answered <\s>
<s> faith i've known a man drink his clar't and drive his coach and four on five hundred a year and strict aconomy in ireland sir <\s>
<s> we'll manage on it sir trust jack costigan for that <\s>
<s> my dear captain costigan i give you my word that my brother did not leave a shilling to his son arthur <\s>
<s> are ye joking with me meejor pendennis <\s>
<s> are ye thrifling with the feelings of a father and a gentleman <\s>
<s> i am telling you the honest truth said major pendennis <\s>
<s> every shilling my brother had he left to his widow with a partial reversion it is true to the boy <\s>
<s> but she is a young woman and may marry if he offends her or she may outlive him for she comes of an uncommonly long lived family <\s>
<s> and i ask you as a gentleman and a man of the world what allowance can my sister mrs <\s>
<s> pendennis make to her son out of five hundred a year which is all her fortune that shall enable him to maintain himself and your daughter in the rank befitting such an accomplished young lady <\s>
<s> am i to understand sir that the young gentleman your nephew and whom i have fosthered and cherished as the son of me bosom is an imposther who has been thrifling with the affections of me beloved child <\s>
<s> exclaimed the general with an outbreak of wrath have you yourself been working upon the feelings of the young man's susceptible nature to injuice him to break off an engagement and with it me adored emily's heart <\s>
<s> have a care sir how you thrifle with the honour of john costigan <\s>
<s> if i thought any mortal man meant to do so be heavens i'd have his blood sir were he old or young <\s>
<s> cried out the major <\s>
<s> costigan can protect his own and his daughter's honour and will sir said the other <\s>
<s> look at that chest of dthrawers it contains heaps of letthers that that viper has addressed to that innocent child <\s>
<s> there's promises there sir enough to fill a bandbox with and when i have dragged the scoundthrel before the courts of law and shown up his perjury and his dishonour i have another remedy in yondther mahogany case sir which shall set me right sir with any individual ye mark me words major pendennis with any individual who has counselled your nephew to insult a soldier and a gentleman <\s>
<s> me daughter to be jilted and me grey hairs dishonoured by an apothecary's son <\s>
<s> by the laws of heaven sir i should like to see the man that shall do it <\s>
<s> i am to understand then that you threaten in the first place to publish the letters of a boy of eighteen to a woman of eight and twenty and afterwards to do me the honour of calling me out the major said still with perfect coolness <\s>
<s> you have described my intentions with perfect accuracy meejor pendennis answered the captain as he pulled his ragged whiskers over his chin <\s>
<s> well well these shall be the subjects of future arrangements but before we come to powder and ball my good sir do have the kindness to think with yourself in what earthly way i have injured you <\s>
<s> i have told you that my nephew is dependent upon his mother who has scarcely more than five hundred a year <\s>
<s> i have my own opinion of the correctness of that assertion said the captain <\s>
<s> will you go to my sister's lawyers messrs <\s>
<s> tatham here and satisfy yourself <\s>
<s> i decline to meet those gentlemen said the captain with rather a disturbed air <\s>
<s> if it be as you say i have been athrociously deceived by some one and on that person i'll be revenged <\s>
<s> is it my nephew <\s>
<s> cried the major starting up and putting on his hat <\s>
<s> did he ever tell you that his property was two thousand a year <\s>
<s> if he did i'm mistaken in the boy <\s>
<s> to tell lies has not been a habit in our family mr <\s>
<s> costigan and i don't think my brother's son has learned it as yet <\s>
<s> try and consider whether you have not deceived yourself or adopted extravagant reports from hearsay as for me sir you are at liberty to understand that i am not afraid of all the costigans in ireland and know quite well how to defend myself against any threats from any quarter <\s>
<s> i come here as the boy's guardian to protest against a marriage most absurd and unequal that cannot but bring poverty and misery with it and in preventing it i conceive i am quite as much your daughter's friend who i have no doubt is an honourable young lady as the friend of my own family and prevent the marriage i will sir by every means in my power <\s>
<s> there i have said my say sir <\s>
<s> but i have not said mine major pendennis and ye shall hear more from me mr <\s>
<s> costigan said with a look of tremendous severity <\s>
<s> sdeath sir what do you mean <\s>
<s> the major asked turning round on the threshold of the door and looking the intrepid costigan in the face <\s>
<s> ye said in the coorse of conversation that ye were at the george hotel i think mr <\s>
<s> costigan said in a stately manner <\s>
<s> a friend shall wait upon ye there before ye leave town sir <\s>
<s> let him make haste mr <\s>
<s> costigan cried out the major almost beside himself with rage <\s>
<s> i wish you a good morning sir <\s>
<s> and captain costigan bowed a magnificent bow of defiance to major pendennis over the landing place as the latter retreated down the stairs <\s>

<s> arthur pendennis and his daughter miss fotheringay and to fix an early day for its celebration or in any other case to give him the satisfaction which was usual between gentlemen of honour <\s>

<s> but captain costigan i can't help smiling at one thing you have just said <\s>
<s> and what's that sir <\s>
<s> asked jack who was at a too heroic and sentimental pitch to descend from it <\s>
<s> you were speaking about our splendid mansion my sister's house i mean <\s>
<s> i mane the park and mansion of arthur pendennis esquire of fairoaks park whom i hope to see a mimber of parliament for his native town of clavering when he is of ege to take that responsible stetion cried the captain with much dignity <\s>
<s> the major smiled as he recognised a shaft of his own bow <\s>
<s> it was he who had set pen upon the idea of sitting in parliament for the neighbouring borough and the poor lad had evidently been bragging on the subject to costigan and the lady of his affections <\s>
<s> fairoaks park my dear sir he said <\s>
<s> do you know our history <\s>
<s> we are of excessively ancient family certainly but i began life with scarce enough money to purchase my commission and my eldest brother was a country apothecary who made every shilling he died possessed of out of his pestle and mortar <\s>
<s> i have consented to waive that objection sir said costigan majestically in consideration of the known respectability of your family <\s>
<s> curse your impudence thought the major but he only smiled and bowed <\s>
<s> the costigans too have met with misfortunes and our house of castle costigan is by no manes what it was <\s>
<s> i have known very honest men apothecaries sir and there's some in dublin that has had the honour of dining at the lord leftenant's teeble <\s>
<s> you are very kind to give us the benefit of your charity the major continued but permit me to say that is not the question <\s>
<s> you spoke just now of my little nephew as heir of fairoaks park and i don't know what besides <\s>
<s> funded property i've no doubt meejor and something handsome eventually from yourself <\s>
<s> my good sir i tell you the boy is the son of a country apothecary cried out major pendennis and that when he comes of age he won't have a shilling <\s>
<s> pooh major you're laughing at me said mr <\s>
<s> costigan me young friend i make no doubt is heir to two thousand pounds a year <\s>
<s> i beg your pardon my dear sir but has the boy been humbugging you it is not his habit <\s>
<s> upon my word and honour as a gentleman and an executor to my brother's will too he left little more than five hundred a year behind him <\s>
<s> and with aconomy a handsome sum of money too sir the captain answered <\s>
<s> faith i've known a man drink his clar't and drive his coach and four on five hundred a year and strict aconomy in ireland sir <\s>
<s> we'll manage on it sir trust jack costigan for that <\s>
<s> my dear captain costigan i give you my word that my brother did not leave a shilling to his son arthur <\s>
<s> are ye joking with me meejor pendennis <\s>
<s> are ye thrifling with the feelings of a father and a gentleman <\s>
<s> i am telling you the honest truth said major pendennis <\s>
<s> every shilling my brother had he left to his widow with a partial reversion it is true to the boy <\s>
<s> but she is a young woman and may marry if he offends her or she may outlive him for she comes of an uncommonly long lived family <\s>
<s> and i ask you as a gentleman and a man of the world what allowance can my sister mrs <\s>
<s> pendennis make to her son out of five hundred a year which is all her fortune that shall enable him to maintain himself and your daughter in the rank befitting such an accomplished young lady <\s>
<s> am i to understand sir that the young gentleman your nephew and whom i have fosthered and cherished as the son of me bosom is an imposther who has been thrifling with the affections of me beloved child <\s>
<s> exclaimed the general with an outbreak of wrath have you yourself been working upon the feelings of the young man's susceptible nature to injuice him to break off an engagement and with it me adored emily's heart <\s>
<s> have a care sir how you thrifle with the honour of john costigan <\s>
<s> if i thought any mortal man meant to do so be heavens i'd have his blood sir were he old or young <\s>
<s> cried out the major <\s>
<s> costigan can protect his own and his daughter's honour and will sir said the other <\s>
<s> look at that chest of dthrawers it contains heaps of letthers that that viper has addressed to that innocent child <\s>
<s> there's promises there sir enough to fill a bandbox with and when i have dragged the scoundthrel before the courts of law and shown up his perjury and his dishonour i have another remedy in yondther mahogany case sir which shall set me right sir with any individual ye mark me words major pendennis with any individual who has counselled your nephew to insult a soldier and a gentleman <\s>
<s> me daughter to be jilted and me grey hairs dishonoured by an apothecary's son <\s>
<s> by the laws of heaven sir i should like to see the man that shall do it <\s>
<s> i am to understand then that you threaten in the first place to publish the letters of a boy of eighteen to a woman of eight and twenty and afterwards to do me the honour of calling me out the major said still with perfect coolness <\s>
<s> you have described my intentions with perfect accuracy meejor pendennis answered the captain as he pulled his ragged whiskers over his chin <\s>
<s> well well these shall be the subjects of future arrangements but before we come to powder and ball my good sir do have the kindness to think with yourself in what earthly way i have injured you <\s>
<s> i have told you that my nephew is dependent upon his mother who has scarcely more than five hundred a year <\s>
<s> i have my own opinion of the correctness of that assertion said the captain <\s>
<s> will you go to my sister's lawyers messrs <\s>
<s> tatham here and satisfy yourself <\s>
<s> i decline to meet those gentlemen said the captain with rather a disturbed air <\s>
<s> if it be as you say i have been athrociously deceived by some one and on that person i'll be revenged <\s>
<s> is it my nephew <\s>
<s> cried the major starting up and putting on his hat <\s>
<s> did he ever tell you that his property was two thousand a year <\s>
<s> if he did i'm mistaken in the boy <\s>
<s> to tell lies has not been a habit in our family mr <\s>
<s> costigan and i don't think my brother's son has learned it as yet <\s>
<s> try and consider whether you have not deceived yourself or adopted extravagant reports from hearsay as for me sir you are at liberty to understand that i am not afraid of all the costigans in ireland and know quite well how to defend myself against any threats from any quarter <\s>
<s> i come here as the boy's guardian to protest against a marriage most absurd and unequal that cannot but bring poverty and misery with it and in preventing it i conceive i am quite as much your daughter's friend who i have no doubt is an honourable young lady as the friend of my own family and prevent the marriage i will sir by every means in my power <\s>
<s> there i have said my say sir <\s>
<s> but i have not said mine major pendennis and ye shall hear more from me mr <\s>
<s> costigan said with a look of tremendous severity <\s>
<s> sdeath sir what do you mean <\s>

<s> ye said in the coorse of conversation that ye were at the george hotel i think mr <\s>
<s> costigan said in a stately manner <\s>
<s> a friend shall wait upon ye there before ye leave town sir <\s>
<s> let him make haste mr <\s>
<s> costigan cried out the major almost beside himself with rage <\s>
<s> i wish you a good morning sir <\s>
<s> and captain costigan bowed a magnificent bow of defiance to major pendennis over the landing place as the latter retreated down the stairs <\s>

<s> arthur pendennis and his daughter miss fotheringay and to fix an early day for its celebration or in any other case to give him the satisfaction which was usual between gentlemen of honour <\s>

<s> i come here as the boy's guardian to protest against a marriage most absurd and unequal that cannot but bring poverty and misery with it and in preventing it i conceive i am quite as much your daughter's friend who i have no doubt is an honourable young lady as the friend of my own family and prevent the marriage i will sir by every means in my power <\s>

<s> captain costigan did not disclose to him the whole of the previous events of which the reader is in possession but with the aid of the spirits and water he composed a letter of a threatening nature to major pendennis's address in which he called upon that gentleman to offer no hindrance to the marriage projected between mr <\s>
<s> arthur pendennis and his daughter miss fotheringay and to fix an early day for its celebration or in any other case to give him the satisfaction which was usual between gentlemen of honour <\s>
<s> and should major pendennis be disinclined to this alternative the captain hinted that he would force him to accept by the use of a horsewhip which he should employ upon the major's person <\s>
<s> the precise terms of this letter we cannot give for reasons which shall be specified presently but it was no doubt couched in the captain's finest style and sealed elaborately with the great silver seal of the costigans the only bit of the family plate which the captain possessed <\s>
<s> garbetts was despatched then with this message and letter and bidding heaven bless um the general squeezed his ambassador's hand and saw him depart <\s>
<s> then he took down his venerable and murderous duelling pistols with flint locks that had done the business of many a pretty fellow in dublin and having examined these and seen that they were in a satisfactory condition he brought from the drawer all pen's letters and poems which he kept there and which he always read before he permitted his emily to enjoy their perusal <\s>

<s> asked jack who was at a too heroic and sentimental pitch to descend from it <\s>
<s> you were speaking about our splendid mansion my sister's house i mean <\s>

<s> fairoaks park my dear sir he said <\s>
<s> do you know our history <\s>
<s> we are of excessively ancient family certainly but i began life with scarce enough money to purchase my commission and my eldest brother was a country apothecary who made every shilling he died possessed of out of his pestle and mortar <\s>
<s> i have consented to waive that objection sir said costigan majestically in consideration of the known respectability of your family <\s>
<s> curse your impudence thought the major but he only smiled and bowed <\s>
<s> the costigans too have met with misfortunes and our house of castle costigan is by no manes what it was <\s>
<s> i have known very honest men apothecaries sir and there's some in dublin that has had the honour of dining at the lord leftenant's teeble <\s>
<s> you are very kind to give us the benefit of your charity the major continued but permit me to say that is not the question <\s>

<s> pooh major you're laughing at me said mr <\s>

<s> pendennis make to her son out of five hundred a year which is all her fortune that shall enable him to maintain himself and your daughter in the rank befitting such an accomplished young lady <\s>

<s> i have consented to waive that objection sir said costigan majestically in consideration of the known respectability of your family <\s>
<s> curse your impudence thought the major but he only smiled and bowed <\s>
<s> the costigans too have met with misfortunes and our house of castle costigan is by no manes what it was <\s>
<s> i have known very honest men apothecaries sir and there's some in dublin that has had the honour of dining at the lord leftenant's teeble <\s>
<s> you are very kind to give us the benefit of your charity the major continued but permit me to say that is not the question <\s>
<s> you spoke just now of my little nephew as heir of fairoaks park and i don't know what besides <\s>
<s> funded property i've no doubt meejor and something handsome eventually from yourself <\s>
<s> my good sir i tell you the boy is the son of a country apothecary cried out major pendennis and that when he comes of age he won't have a shilling <\s>
<s> pooh major you're laughing at me said mr <\s>
<s> costigan me young friend i make no doubt is heir to two thousand pounds a year <\s>
<s> i beg your pardon my dear sir but has the boy been humbugging you it is not his habit <\s>
<s> upon my word and honour as a gentleman and an executor to my brother's will too he left little more than five hundred a year behind him <\s>
<s> and with aconomy a handsome sum of money too sir the captain answered <\s>
<s> faith i've known a man drink his clar't and drive his coach and four on five hundred a year and strict aconomy in ireland sir <\s>
<s> we'll manage on it sir trust jack costigan for that <\s>
<s> my dear captain costigan i give you my word that my brother did not leave a shilling to his son arthur <\s>
<s> are ye joking with me meejor pendennis <\s>
<s> are ye thrifling with the feelings of a father and a gentleman <\s>
<s> i am telling you the honest truth said major pendennis <\s>
<s> every shilling my brother had he left to his widow with a partial reversion it is true to the boy <\s>
<s> but she is a young woman and may marry if he offends her or she may outlive him for she comes of an uncommonly long lived family <\s>
<s> and i ask you as a gentleman and a man of the world what allowance can my sister mrs <\s>
<s> pendennis make to her son out of five hundred a year which is all her fortune that shall enable him to maintain himself and your daughter in the rank befitting such an accomplished young lady <\s>
<s> am i to understand sir that the young gentleman your nephew and whom i have fosthered and cherished as the son of me bosom is an imposther who has been thrifling with the affections of me beloved child <\s>
<s> exclaimed the general with an outbreak of wrath have you yourself been working upon the feelings of the young man's susceptible nature to injuice him to break off an engagement and with it me adored emily's heart <\s>
<s> have a care sir how you thrifle with the honour of john costigan <\s>
<s> if i thought any mortal man meant to do so be heavens i'd have his blood sir were he old or young <\s>
<s> cried out the major <\s>
<s> costigan can protect his own and his daughter's honour and will sir said the other <\s>
<s> look at that chest of dthrawers it contains heaps of letthers that that viper has addressed to that innocent child <\s>
<s> there's promises there sir enough to fill a bandbox with and when i have dragged the scoundthrel before the courts of law and shown up his perjury and his dishonour i have another remedy in yondther mahogany case sir which shall set me right sir with any individual ye mark me words major pendennis with any individual who has counselled your nephew to insult a soldier and a gentleman <\s>
<s> me daughter to be jilted and me grey hairs dishonoured by an apothecary's son <\s>
<s> by the laws of heaven sir i should like to see the man that shall do it <\s>
<s> i am to understand then that you threaten in the first place to publish the letters of a boy of eighteen to a woman of eight and twenty and afterwards to do me the honour of calling me out the major said still with perfect coolness <\s>
<s> you have described my intentions with perfect accuracy meejor pendennis answered the captain as he pulled his ragged whiskers over his chin <\s>
<s> well well these shall be the subjects of future arrangements but before we come to powder and ball my good sir do have the kindness to think with yourself in what earthly way i have injured you <\s>
<s> i have told you that my nephew is dependent upon his mother who has scarcely more than five hundred a year <\s>
<s> i have my own opinion of the correctness of that assertion said the captain <\s>
<s> will you go to my sister's lawyers messrs <\s>
<s> tatham here and satisfy yourself <\s>
<s> i decline to meet those gentlemen said the captain with rather a disturbed air <\s>
<s> if it be as you say i have been athrociously deceived by some one and on that person i'll be revenged <\s>
<s> is it my nephew <\s>
<s> cried the major starting up and putting on his hat <\s>
<s> did he ever tell you that his property was two thousand a year <\s>
<s> if he did i'm mistaken in the boy <\s>
<s> to tell lies has not been a habit in our family mr <\s>
<s> costigan and i don't think my brother's son has learned it as yet <\s>
<s> try and consider whether you have not deceived yourself or adopted extravagant reports from hearsay as for me sir you are at liberty to understand that i am not afraid of all the costigans in ireland and know quite well how to defend myself against any threats from any quarter <\s>
<s> i come here as the boy's guardian to protest against a marriage most absurd and unequal that cannot but bring poverty and misery with it and in preventing it i conceive i am quite as much your daughter's friend who i have no doubt is an honourable young lady as the friend of my own family and prevent the marriage i will sir by every means in my power <\s>
<s> there i have said my say sir <\s>
<s> but i have not said mine major pendennis and ye shall hear more from me mr <\s>
<s> costigan said with a look of tremendous severity <\s>
<s> sdeath sir what do you mean <\s>
<s> the major asked turning round on the threshold of the door and looking the intrepid costigan in the face <\s>
<s> ye said in the coorse of conversation that ye were at the george hotel i think mr <\s>
<s> costigan said in a stately manner <\s>
<s> a friend shall wait upon ye there before ye leave town sir <\s>
<s> let him make haste mr <\s>
<s> costigan cried out the major almost beside himself with rage <\s>
<s> i wish you a good morning sir <\s>
<s> and captain costigan bowed a magnificent bow of defiance to major pendennis over the landing place as the latter retreated down the stairs <\s>
<s> in which a shooting match is proposed early mention has been made in this history of mr <\s>
<s> garbetts principal tragedian a promising and athletic young actor of jovial habits and irregular inclinations between whom and mr <\s>
<s> costigan there was a considerable intimacy <\s>
<s> they were the chief ornaments of the convivial club held at the magpie hotel they helped each other in various bill transactions in which they had been engaged with the mutual loan of each other's valuable signatures <\s>
<s> they were friends in fine although mr <\s>
<s> garbetts seldom called at costigan's house being disliked by miss fotheringay of whom in her turn mrs <\s>
<s> garbetts was considerably jealous <\s>
<s> the truth is that garbetts had paid his court to miss fotheringay and been refused by her before he offered his hand to mrs <\s>
<s> their history however forms no part of our present scheme suffice it mr <\s>
<s> garbetts was called in by captain costigan immediately after his daughter and mr <\s>
<s> bows had quitted the house as a friend proper to be consulted at the actual juncture <\s>
<s> he was a large man with a loud voice and fierce aspect who had the finest legs of the whole company and could break a poker in mere sport across his stalwart arm <\s>

<s> costigan to the little messenger and fetch mr <\s>

<s> garbetts and the whisky came <\s>
<s> captain costigan did not disclose to him the whole of the previous events of which the reader is in possession but with the aid of the spirits and water he composed a letter of a threatening nature to major pendennis's address in which he called upon that gentleman to offer no hindrance to the marriage projected between mr <\s>
<s> arthur pendennis and his daughter miss fotheringay and to fix an early day for its celebration or in any other case to give him the satisfaction which was usual between gentlemen of honour <\s>
<s> and should major pendennis be disinclined to this alternative the captain hinted that he would force him to accept by the use of a horsewhip which he should employ upon the major's person <\s>
<s> the precise terms of this letter we cannot give for reasons which shall be specified presently but it was no doubt couched in the captain's finest style and sealed elaborately with the great silver seal of the costigans the only bit of the family plate which the captain possessed <\s>
<s> garbetts was despatched then with this message and letter and bidding heaven bless um the general squeezed his ambassador's hand and saw him depart <\s>
<s> then he took down his venerable and murderous duelling pistols with flint locks that had done the business of many a pretty fellow in dublin and having examined these and seen that they were in a satisfactory condition he brought from the drawer all pen's letters and poems which he kept there and which he always read before he permitted his emily to enjoy their perusal <\s>
